```javascript
    elements.favoriteBtn.classList.toggle('active');
    const isFavorite = elements.favoriteBtn.classList.contains('active');
    showToast(isFavorite ? 'Added to favorites' : 'Removed from favorites', 'heart');
  }

  function updateFavoriteState() {
    // Check if track is in favorites
    // elements.favoriteBtn.classList.add('active');
  }

  /* ============================================
     MODAL
  ============================================= */
  
  function openModal(type, content) {
    elements.modalOverlay.classList.add('active');
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    
    if (type === 'lyrics') {
      elements.modalHeaderText.innerHTML = `<i class="fa-solid fa-music"></i> Sözler`;
      elements.modalIframe.style.display = 'none';
      elements.modalLyrics.style.display = 'block';
      elements.modalLyrics.querySelector('.lyrics-content').innerHTML = `
        <p>Seninle her şey güzel</p>
        <p>Seninle zaman duruyor</p>
        <p>Her bakışında</p>
        <p>Dünya güzelleşiyor</p>
        <br>
        <p>Sensiz olmuyor</p>
        <p>Sensiz yaşanmıyor</p>
        <p>Sen benim şarkımın</p>
        <p>En güzel melodisi</p>
      `;
    } else if (type === 'playlist') {
      elements.modalHeaderText.innerHTML = `<i class="fa-solid fa-list"></i> Playlist`;
      elements.modalIframe.style.display = 'none';
      elements.modalLyrics.style.display = 'none';
      elements.modalOverlay.querySelector('.modal-content').innerHTML = `
        <button class="modal-close"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark"></i></button>
        <div class="modal-header-text">
          <i class="fa-solid fa-list"></i> Playlist
        </div>
        <div class="lyrics-content" style="text-align: left; padding: 24px;">
          ${player.playlist.map((track, index) => `
            <div class="top-item" onclick="playTrackFromPlaylist(${index})" style="cursor: pointer;">
              <div class="top-rank">${index + 1}</div>
              <img src="${track.cover}" alt="${track.title}" class="top-thumb">
              <div class="top-info">
                <div class="top-song">${track.title}</div>
                <div class="top-artist">${track.artist}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="top-play-btn">
                <i class="fa-solid fa-play"></i>
              </div>
            </div>
          `).join('')}
        </div>
      `;
      
      // Re-bind close button
      document.querySelector('.modal-close').addEventListener('click', closeModal);
    }
  }

  function closeModal() {
    elements.modalOverlay.classList.remove('active');
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
  }

  /* ============================================
     RECENT TRACKS
  ============================================= */
  
  function renderRecentTracks() {
    if (!elements.recentTracks) return;
    
    elements.recentTracks.innerHTML = player.playlist.map((track, index) => `
      <div class="recent-track-card" onclick="playTrackFromPlaylist(${index})">
        <img src="${track.cover}" alt="${track.title}" class="recent-track-img">
        <div class="recent-track-info">
          <div class="recent-track-title">${track.title}</div>
          <div class="recent-track-artist">${track.artist}</div>
          <div class="recent-track-time">${formatTime(track.duration)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `).join('');
  }

  window.playTrackFromPlaylist = function(index) {
    player.currentTrack = index;
    loadTrack(player.currentTrack);
    playTrack();
  };

  /* ============================================
     SEARCH
  ============================================= */
  
  function handleSearch(e) {
    const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
    
    if (query.length < 2) {
      elements.searchResults.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    
    const results = player.playlist.filter(track => 
      track.title.toLowerCase().includes(query) || 
      track.artist.toLowerCase().includes(query)
    );
    
    if (results.length > 0) {
      elements.searchResults.innerHTML = results.map(track => `
        <div class="top-item" onclick="playTrackFromPlaylist(${player.playlist.indexOf(track)})">
          <img src="${track.cover}" alt="${track.title}" class="top-thumb">
          <div class="top-info">
            <div class="top-song">${track.title}</div>
            <div class="top-artist">${track.artist}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      `).join('');
      elements.searchResults.style.display = 'block';
    } else {
      elements.searchResults.innerHTML = '<div style="padding: 20px; text-align: center; color: var(--text-secondary);">Şarkı bulunamadı</div>';
      elements.searchResults.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }

  function hideSearchResults() {
    setTimeout(() => {
      elements.searchResults.style.display = 'none';
    }, 200);
  }

  /* ============================================
     SCROLL REVEAL
  ============================================= */
  
  function handleScrollReveal() {
    const windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
    
    elements.revealElements.forEach(element => {
      const elementTop = element.getBoundingClientRect().top;
      const revealPoint = 150;
      
      if (elementTop < windowHeight - revealPoint) {
        element.classList.add('active');
      }
    });
  }

  /* ============================================
     CAROUSEL / SLIDER
  ============================================= */
  
  function initCarousel() {
    const slider = document.querySelector('.slider-box .owl-carousel');
    if (!slider) return;
    
    // If Owl Carousel is loaded
    if (typeof $ !== 'undefined' && $.fn.owlCarousel) {
      $(slider).owlCarousel({
        loop: true,
        margin: 0,
        nav: true,
        dots: false,
        autoplay: true,
        autoplayTimeout: 5000,
        autoplayHoverPause: true,
        smartSpeed: 500,
        navSpeed: 500,
        items: 1,
        animateOut: 'fadeOut',
        animateIn: 'fadeIn',
        navText: ['<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-left"></i>', '<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right"></i>']
      });
    } else {
      // Simple fallback slider
      createSimpleSlider();
    }
  }

  function createSimpleSlider() {
    const slider = document.querySelector('.slider-box');
    if (!slider) return;
    
    const slides = [
      { img: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1470225620780-dba8ba36b745?w=1200', title: 'Canlı Yayın', subtitle: 'DJ Mithat ile gece boyunca müzik' },
      { img: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1493225457124-a3eb161ffa5f?w=1200', title: 'Yeni Çıkanlar', subtitle: 'En yeni şarkılar sizin için' },
      { img: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1514525253440-b393452e8d26?w=1200', title: 'Top 40', subtitle: 'Bu haftanın en popüler şarkıları' }
    ];
    
    let currentSlide = 0;
    
    slider.innerHTML = `
      <div class="slider-container" style="position: relative; height: 500px; overflow: hidden;">
        <div class="slides-wrapper" style="display: flex; transition: transform 0.5s ease;"></div>
        <div class="slider-nav" style="position: absolute; bottom: 40px; left: 50%; transform: translateX(-50%); display: flex; gap: 12px; z-index: 10;"></div>
      </div>
    `;
    
    const wrapper = slider.querySelector('.slides-wrapper');
    const nav = slider.querySelector('.slider-nav');
    
    slides.forEach((slide, index) => {
      wrapper.innerHTML += `
        <div class="slide" style="min-width: 100%; height: 500px; position: relative;">
          <img src="${slide.img}" style="width: 100%; height: 100%; object-fit: cover;">
          <div style="position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; right: 0; bottom: 0; background: linear-gradient(to top, rgba(0,0,0,0.8), transparent 50%); display: flex; flex-direction: column; justify-content: flex-end; padding: 60px;">
            <h2 style="font-size: 48px; font-weight: 800; margin-bottom: 12px; color: white;">${slide.title}</h2>
            <p style="font-size: 18px; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.8);">${slide.subtitle}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
      
      nav.innerHTML += `<button class="slide-dot" data-index="${index}" style="width: 12px; height: 12px; border-radius: 50%; border: 2px solid white; background: transparent; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.3s;"></button>`;
    });
    
    nav.querySelectorAll('.slide-dot').forEach(dot => {
      dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
        currentSlide = parseInt(dot.dataset.index);
        updateSlider();
      });
    });
    
    function updateSlider() {
      wrapper.style.transform = `translateX(-${currentSlide * 100}%)`;
      nav.querySelectorAll('.slide-dot').forEach((dot, i) => {
        dot.style.background = i === currentSlide ? 'white' : 'transparent';
      });
    }
    
    // Initialize
    updateSlider();
    
    // Auto advance
    setInterval(() => {
      currentSlide = (currentSlide + 1) % slides.length;
      updateSlider();
    }, 5000);
  }

  /* ============================================
     EVENT LISTENERS
  ============================================= */
  
  function initEventListeners() {
    // Header scroll
    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleHeaderScroll);
    
    // Theme toggle
    elements.themeToggle.addEventListener('click', toggleTheme);
    
    // Mobile menu
    elements.menuToggle.addEventListener('click', toggleMobileMenu);
    elements.mobileClose.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);
    elements.mobileNavLinks.forEach(link => {
      link.addEventListener('click', closeMobileMenu);
    });
    
    // Notification dropdown
    elements.notificationBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleNotificationDropdown);
    
    // Close dropdowns on outside click
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      if (!e.target.closest('.notification-dropdown') && !e.target.closest('.notification-btn')) {
        elements.notificationDropdown.classList.remove('active');
      }
      if (!e.target.closest('.chat-panel') && !e.target.closest('.chat-toggle-btn')) {
        elements.chatPanel.classList.remove('active');
      }
    });
    
    // Chat panel
    elements.chatToggleBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleChatPanel);
    elements.chatClose.addEventListener('click', toggleChatPanel);
    elements.chatInput.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') sendChatMessage();
    });
    
    // Player controls
    elements.playBtn.addEventListener('click', togglePlay);
    elements.prevBtn.addEventListener('click', prevTrack);
    elements.nextBtn.addEventListener('click', nextTrack);
    elements.floatingPlayBtn.addEventListener('click', togglePlay);
    
    // Volume
    elements.volumeRange.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
      setVolume(e.target.value);
    });
    
    // Equalizer
    elements.equalizerBtns.forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        setEqualizer(btn.dataset.eq);
      });
    });
    
    // Lyrics button
    if (elements.lyricsBtn) {
      elements.lyricsBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        openModal('lyrics');
      });
    }
    
    // Favorite button
    if (elements.favoriteBtn) {
      elements.favoriteBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleFavorite);
    }
    
    // Modal
    if (elements.modalClose) {
      elements.modalClose.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
    }
    if (elements.modalOverlay) {
      elements.modalOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (e.target === elements.modalOverlay) closeModal();
      });
    }
    
    // Progress ring click
    if (elements.circleWrap) {
      elements.circleWrap.addEventListener('click', handleProgressClick);
    }
    
    // Search
    if (elements.searchInput) {
      elements.searchInput.addEventListener('input', handleSearch);
      elements.searchInput.addEventListener('blur', hideSearchResults);
    }
    
    // Scroll reveal
    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScrollReveal);
    handleScrollReveal(); // Initial check
    
    // Keyboard shortcuts
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.target.tagName === 'INPUT' || e.target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') return;
      
      switch(e.code) {
        case 'Space':
          e.preventDefault();
          togglePlay();
          break;
        case 'ArrowLeft':
          prevTrack();
          break;
        case 'ArrowRight':
          nextTrack();
          break;
        case 'KeyM':
          setVolume(player.volume > 0 ? 0 : 80);
          break;
        case 'Escape':
          closeMobileMenu();
          closeModal();
          elements.notificationDropdown.classList.remove('active');
          elements.chatPanel.classList.remove('active');
          break;
      }
    });
  }

  /* ============================================
     INITIALIZATION
  ============================================= */
  
  function init() {
    cacheElements();
    initEventListeners();
    loadTrack(0);
    renderRecentTracks();
    initCarousel();
    
    // Load saved theme
    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') || 'dark';
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', savedTheme);
    
    const themeIcon = elements.themeToggle.querySelector('i');
    if (themeIcon) {
      themeIcon.className = savedTheme === 'light' ? 'fa-solid fa-moon' : 'fa-solid fa-sun';
    }
    
    // Set volume
    setVolume(player.volume * 100);
    
    console.log('🎵 ZenFM Radio Player initialized');
  }

  // Start the application
  init();
});
</script>
```

---

## 📋 Kullanım Talimatları

### HTML Dosyası Oluşturma:

```bash
# index.html dosyası oluştur
touch index.html

# Kodları dosyaya yapıştır
```

### Gerekli Dosyalar:
- **Font Awesome** - İkonlar için (CDN otomatik dahil)
- **Owl Carousel** - Sliders için (CDN otomatik dahil)

### Özellikler:
✅ Modern gradient tasarım  
✅ Tam duyarlı (Responsive)  
✅ Dark/Light tema desteği  
✅ Canlı ses akışı  
✅ Gerçekçi görselleştirici  
✅ Sohbet paneli  
✅ Bildirim sistemi  
✅ Mobil menü  
✅ Klavye kısayolları (Space, ←, →, M, Esc)  
✅ Çevrimdışı destekli yapı  

Herhangi bir sorunuz varsa yardımcı olabilirim! 🎶
